    $(document).ready(function () {

        var activeMenuId = $('.g-menu-level[data-menu="' + window.HSG.Config.ActiveMenuId + '"]');
        
        if (activeMenuId) {
            activeMenuId.addClass('e-active');
        }

        var activeId = $('.e-menu-item-link[data-id="' + window.HSG.Config.ActiveId + '"]');

        if (activeId) {
            activeId.addClass('e-active');
        }

        for (var i = 0; i < window.HSG.Config.ActiveMainMenuIds.length; i++)
        {
            var activeMainMenuId = $('li[data-id="' + window.HSG.Config.ActiveMainMenuIds[i] + '"]');

            if (activeMainMenuId) {
                activeMainMenuId.addClass('e-trail');
                activeMainMenuId.attr("data-trail", "1");
            }
        }

		var application = new T.Application();
		application.registerModules();
		application.registerModule(document.createElement('div'), 'PageController');
		application.start();

        // enable routing
		$(window).trigger('hashchange');
	});
